var focusastig_corrected=newArray(0,0,0,0,0,0),globmeans=newArray(6),deletewd,A,B,C,D,a,b,c,a2,b2,c2,a3,b3,c3,opty,opty1,opty2,opty3,globemailrecipient=newArray("brainmaps@gmail.com"),
emailstr="",wd_old,wd_new,wd_step=0.001,wd,astigx,astigy,tilecount,wd_offset=0,wd_offset_gain=1;

macro "acquire beamshift"{
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y"); wait(100);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X"); wait(100);
}


macro "acquire focus points [F6]"
{
//try using store resolution = 2048x1536, pixel size = 80nm, I Probe = 5nA, EHT = 0.8kV, scan speed = 5, WD = 3.9mm

	var focuspass=0,DP_AUTO,wd,wd_start,beamshifty,beamshiftx,w,i,j,k,astigx,astigy, numfocuspoints=40,nonoverlap=0.9, xcount,ycount,width,height,waittime,scandirection,deltaX,deltaY,filename,stagemovetime=300,xPoshold, yPoshold,passthru=0,wd_old,tryautofocus=0,gotostart=0,autofocuscount=1,turnoffEHT=1,freqrandpoints=0.25,wd_start=3.861,xPos0,yPos0,randjit=1/20000;
	var scantype=0;  // 0 = L->R, D, R->L,   1 = R -> L, D, R ->L
	var usehexgrid=1; //use hexagonal grid of focus points
	var hexspacing=2.0;  //hexagonal grid spacing in mm
	var wdmin=3 , wdmax=4.5;
	wd_start=3.9;
	var dryrun=0;
	
	
	var xtiles=0, ytiles=0;  //set xtiles to zero to use bounding box instead
	box= newArray(60.54,66.037,68.123,54.482);    //bounding box:  top, left, bottom, right
	//boxfocuspoints= newArray(61.84,66.45,66.55,59.57 ); //bounding box:  top, left, bottom, right
	//z 18.077 t 0.5 r 136.9
	boxfocuspoints= box;
	
	run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(2000);
	
	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y"); wait(100);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X"); wait(100);	
beamshifty=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y", nResults-1);	
beamshiftx=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_X", nResults-1);	

//print("BEAMSHIFT: "+beamshiftx + " " +beamshifty);

 
	
	 
	
	 
		var hexnumx1,hexnumx2,hexnumy1,hexnumy2,hexcount;
		hexnumx1=floor((box[1]-box[3])/(hexspacing))+1; 
		hexnumy1=floor((box[2]-box[0])/hexspacing)+1; 
		hextotal=hexnumx1*hexnumy1;
		print("HEXTOTAL " +hextotal);
			focuspoints= newArray(hextotal*4); 
		hexcount=0;
		for(i=1;i<=hexnumx1;i=i+1){		
		for(j=1;j<=hexnumy1;j=j+1){		
			hexcount=hexcount+1;
			xPos0=(boxfocuspoints[1]-hexspacing*(i-1))/1000+randjit*random;
			yPos0=(boxfocuspoints[0]+hexspacing*(j-1))/1000+randjit*random;
			if (dryrun==0){
			run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_GOTO_X "+xPos0); wait(500);
			run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_GOTO_Y "+yPos0); wait(500);
			wait(stagemovetime+300);
			run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshifty); wait(100);	
			run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftx); wait(100);	
			
			//run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd_start); wait(200);
			run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v ");
			wd_old=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);	
			wait(100);
			run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 0");
			wait(100);
			focuspointpause();
			//run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_AUTO_FOCUS_FINE"); 
			//print(hexcount+" waitstart"); 
			//wait(60000);
			//print(hexcount+" waitend");
			
			run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1");	wait(100);

	run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v ");
	run("SEM ", "GetStigmator v"); 
	run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_X");wait(50);
	run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_Y");wait(50);

	wd=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);
	astigx=getResult("StigX", nResults-1);
	astigy=getResult("StigY", nResults-1);
	xPos=getResult("AP_STAGE_AT_X", nResults-1);
	yPos=getResult("AP_STAGE_AT_Y", nResults-1);
			
			if(deletewd==false){
				print(1000*xPos+ ", "+1000*yPos+ ", "+wd+", "+astigx+", "+astigy);
				focuspass=1;
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)]=1000*xPos; 
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)+1]=1000*yPos;
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)+2]=wd;
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)+3]=0;
			}else{
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)]=0; 
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)+1]=0;
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)+2]=wd;
				focuspoints[4*(hexcount-1)+3]=0;
				}
				
				
					}else{
			print(xPos0*1000+" "+yPos0*1000);
		}
			
			
			}
			
			
			
	
			}
			
			  
			
			}















macro "stage movement test"
{
//try using store resolution = 2048x1536, pixel size = 80nm, I Probe = 5nA, EHT = 0.8kV, scan speed = 5, WD = 3.9mm

	var focuspass=0,DP_AUTO,wd,wd_start,beamshifty,beamshiftx,w,i,j,k,astigx,astigy, numfocuspoints=40,nonoverlap=0.9, xcount,ycount,width,height,waittime,scandirection,deltaX,deltaY,filename,stagemovetime=300,xPoshold, yPoshold,passthru=0,wd_old,tryautofocus=0,gotostart=0,autofocuscount=1,turnoffEHT=1,freqrandpoints=0.25,wd_start=3.861,xPos0,yPos0,randjit=1/20000;
	var scantype=0;  // 0 = L->R, D, R->L,   1 = R -> L, D, R ->L
	var usehexgrid=1; //use hexagonal grid of focus points
	var hexspacing=1;  //hexagonal grid spacing in mm

	run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_X");wait(50);
	run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_Y");wait(50);			 
			xPos=getResult("AP_STAGE_AT_X", nResults-1); 
			yPos=getResult("AP_STAGE_AT_Y", nResults-1);			
			//print(xPos0*1000+" "+xPos*1000 +" " +yPos0*1000+" "+yPos*1000);
			print("ACTUAL POSITION: " +xPos*1000+" "+yPos*1000);
		
			
			
			}
			
			
			
	
			}

		}else{

			*/
	//}

	run("SEM ", "GetStigmator v");

	astigy=getResult("StigY", nResults-1);

	width=getResult("AP_WIDTH", nResults-1);
	height=getResult("AP_HEIGHT", nResults-1);
	
	if (xtiles==0){

		ytiles=floor((box[2]-box[0])/(height*nonoverlap*1000))+1;
		}
		print(xtiles+ " " + ytiles);

	if (drawannotations==1){

	}else{
	newImage("overview", "8-bit White", OVwidth, OVheight, 1);
	}
	
	for(ycount=0;ycount<ytiles;ycount=ycount+1){
		for(xcount=0;xcount<xtiles;xcount=xcount+1){
					run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_X");wait(50);
			run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_Y");wait(50);

					scandirection=-1;

				}
			}else{

				}

			 wait(80);

				deltaY=0;
				wait(100);
				//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_Y "+0); wait(100);
				run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_X "+deltaX);  wait(100);
				run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_X "+0);  
				print("xmoved "+(-scandirection*width));
			}else{
				//print("calculated: "+xPos +" " +yPos+height*nonoverlap);
				//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_GOTO_Y "+yPos+height*nonoverlap);

				deltaY=height*nonoverlap;
				//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_X "+0); wait(100);
				wait(100);
				run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_Y "+deltaY);  wait(200);
				run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_Y "+0);   wait(100);
				if(scantype==1){
				//print("BIG MOVE");
					deltaX=-scandirection*width*nonoverlap; wait(100);
					run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_X "+-deltaX*(xtiles-1));  wait(1000);
					run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_DELTA_X "+0); wait(100);
				}
				//print("ymoved "+height);
			}
			wait(100);
			//print(filename+" " + deltaX+" " + deltaY);
			
			run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_X");wait(50);
			run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_STAGE_AT_Y");wait(50);
			xPos=getResult("AP_STAGE_AT_X", nResults-1);
			yPos=getResult("AP_STAGE_AT_Y", nResults-1);
			
			 
			 
	
open(dirname+filename);
//run("Subtract Background...", "rolling=50 light");
//run("Subtract Background...", "rolling=100 light disable");

if (drawannotations==1){

setColor(0, 255,0);
setFont("SansSerif", 70, "antialiased");

if(scandirection==1){

}else{

	}

macro "autofocus test "
{
var wd_old,wd_new,wd_step=0.001,dirnamewd="D:\\Test\\",waittimewd,width,height,std1,std2;


run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(2000);
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y"); wait(100);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X"); wait(100);	
wd_old=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);	
wd_new=wd_old+wd_step;
beamshifty=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y", nResults-1);	
beamshiftx=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_X", nResults-1);	

run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_FRAME_TIME");
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_WIDTH");
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_HEIGHT");
waittimewd=1.1*getResult("AP_FRAME_TIME", nResults-1);
width=getResult("AP_WIDTH", nResults-1);
height=getResult("AP_HEIGHT", nResults-1);

compareFocus(wd_old,wd_new);
//print(wd_new + " " +wd_old+ " " +std1+" "+std2);
 
while (std1<std2){
wd_old=wd_new;
wd_new=wd_new+wd_step;
compareFocus(wd_old,wd_new);
print(wd_new + " " +wd_old+ " " +std1+" "+std2);
}
while (std1>std2){
wd_new=wd_old;
wd_old=wd_old-wd_step;
compareFocus(wd_old,wd_new);
print(wd_new + " " +wd_old+ " " +std1+" "+std2);
}

run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 2"); wait(100);

}








function compareFocus(wd_old,wd_new){


run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd_old); wait(200);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 1"); wait(100);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); wait(100);

run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 0"); wait(100);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); wait(100);
wait(waittimewd+100); 

run("SEM ", "FileSave v "+dirnamewd+"testfocus1.tif");
wait(100);		


run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd_new); wait(100);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 1"); wait(100);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); wait(100);

run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 0"); wait(100);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); wait(100);
wait(waittimewd+100); 

run("SEM ", "FileSave v "+dirnamewd+"testfocus2.tif");
wait(100);		

open("D:\\Test\\testfocus1.tif");
open("D:\\Test\\testfocus2.tif");
selectWindow("testfocus1.tif");
run("Median...", "radius=0.5");
selectWindow("testfocus2.tif");
run("Median...", "radius=0.5");
selectWindow("testfocus1.tif");
getStatistics(mean,std);
std1=std;
close();
selectWindow("testfocus2.tif");
getStatistics(mean,std);
std2=std;
close();


}











macro "autofocusGradientDescent test"{
	

	
 run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y");  
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X");  
beamshifty=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y", nResults-1);	
beamshiftx=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_X", nResults-1);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v DP_SCANRATE"); wait(50);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE1");
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 2770");
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 1"); 
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_FRAME_TIME");

waittimewd=1.1*getResult("AP_FRAME_TIME", nResults-1);
scanrate=getResult("DP_SCANRATE", nResults-1);



	
setBatchMode(true);

makefocusastigmasks(sisc*6,sisc*0.5,sisc*3,fxxsize);
globmeans[0]=getmean("maskfocusouter");
globmeans[1]=getmean("maskfocusinner");	



run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(10);
wd=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);
wdstart=wd;

wdstep=0.008;

wait(waittimewd+100);
imagename="testfocus0.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
run("SEM ", "FileSave v "+dirimagename);wait(50);
computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
y0=focusnormalized;
imagename="testfocus1.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
acquireimage(wd-wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
y1=focusnormalized;
imagename="testfocus2.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
acquireimage(wd+wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
y2=focusnormalized;


if ((y2-y0)>(y1-y0)){
	while (y2>y0){
		run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(10);
		wd=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);
		y0=y2;
		imagename="testfocus2.tif";
		dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
		acquireimage(wd+wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
		computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
		y2=focusnormalized;
	}
	wd=wd-wdstep;
}else{
	while (y1>y0){
		run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(10);
		wd=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);
		y0=y1;
		imagename="testfocus1.tif";
		dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
		acquireimage(wd-wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
		computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
		y1=focusnormalized;
	}
	wd=wd+wdstep;
}		







wdstep=0.005;

imagename="testfocus0.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
acquireimage(wd,waittimewd,dirimagename);
computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
y0=focusnormalized;
imagename="testfocus1.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
acquireimage(wd-wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
y1=focusnormalized;
imagename="testfocus2.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
acquireimage(wd+wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
y2=focusnormalized;


if ((y2-y0)>(y1-y0)){
	while (y2>y0){
		run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(10);
		wd=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);
		y0=y2;
		imagename="testfocus2.tif";
		dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
		acquireimage(wd+wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
		computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
		y2=focusnormalized;
	}
	wd=wd-wdstep;
}else{
	while (y1>y0){
		run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(10);
		wd=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);
		y0=y1;
		imagename="testfocus1.tif";
		dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
		acquireimage(wd-wdstep,waittimewd,dirimagename);
		computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
		y1=focusnormalized;
	}
	wd=wd+wdstep;
}		








 

	
 

run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshifty); wait(60);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftx); wait(60);	
 
selectWindow("maskxminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskxplus");
close();    
selectWindow("maskyminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskyplus");
close();   
selectWindow("maskfocusinner");
close();
selectWindow("maskfocusouter");
close();

setBatchMode(false);

 


run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE"+scanrate);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 689"); 
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 2"); 


run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd); wait(50);

print(wdstart+" "+wd);
   
 	  
}




























macro "autofocusLS test"{
 run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y");  
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X");  
beamshifty=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y", nResults-1);	
beamshiftx=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_X", nResults-1);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v DP_SCANRATE"); wait(50);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE1");
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 2770");
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 1"); 
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_FRAME_TIME");

waittimewd=1.1*getResult("AP_FRAME_TIME", nResults-1);
scanrate=getResult("DP_SCANRATE", nResults-1);

	
setBatchMode(true);
	


makefocusastigmasks(sisc*6,sisc*0.5,sisc*3,fxxsize);
globmeans[0]=getmean("maskfocusouter");
globmeans[1]=getmean("maskfocusinner");
 


var wd_steps=5; //number of wd steps.  must be odd
var wd_stepsize=0.01; //in mm

x=newArray(wd_steps+1);
y=newArray(wd_steps+1);
y2=newArray(wd_steps+1);
 

//wd=wd_vec[tilecount];
run("SEM ", "GetFreeWorkingDistance v "); wait(10);
wd=getResult("FWD", nResults-1);
 

for(i=1;i<=wd_steps;i=i+1){
	x[i]=wd+(i-(wd_steps+1)/2)*wd_stepsize;
	var imagename="testfocus"+i+".tif";
	var dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
	beamshiftynew=beamshifty+(random-0.5)*1;
	beamshiftxnew=beamshiftx+(random-0.5)*1;
	run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshiftynew);  
	run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftxnew); wait(20);	
	acquireimage(x[i],waittimewd,dirimagename); 
	computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
	y2[i]=computeVarfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
	y[i]=log(focusnormalized);
	if (i==1){
		optwd1x=x[1]; optwd1y=y[1];
	}else{
		if (y[i]>optwd1y){
			optwd1x=x[i]; optwd1y=y[i];
		}
	}
}
 

run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE6");
run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd); wait(100);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshifty); wait(60);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftx); wait(60);	
 
selectWindow("maskxminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskxplus");
close();    
selectWindow("maskyminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskyplus");
close();   
selectWindow("maskfocusinner");
close();
selectWindow("maskfocusouter");
close();

setBatchMode(false);


// http://www.codeproject.com/KB/recipes/QuadraticRegression.aspx

s21=0;s11=0;s01=0;s40=0;s30=0;s20=0;s10=0;s00=0;
for(i=1;i<=wd_steps;i=i+1){
	s21=s21+y[i]*pow(x[i],2);
	s11=s11+y[i]*x[i];
	s01=s01+y[i];
	s40=s40+pow(x[i],4);
	s30=s30+pow(x[i],3);
	s20=s20+pow(x[i],2);
	s10=s10+x[i];	
	s00=s00+1;
}		
D=s40*(s20*s00-s10*s10) - s30*(s30*s00-s10*s20) + s20*(s30*s10-s20*s20);
Da=s21*(s20*s00-s10*s10) - s11*(s30*s00-s10*s20) + s01*(s30*s10-s20*s20);
Db=s40*(s11*s00-s01*s10) - s30*(s21*s00-s01*s20) + s20*(s21*s10-s11*s20);
Dc=s40*(s20*s01-s10*s11) - s30*(s30*s01-s10*s21) + s20*(s30*s11-s20*s21);

a=Da/D;
b=Db/D;
c=Dc/D;

focusastig_corrected[0]=-b/(2*a);
opty = a*pow(focusastig_corrected[0],2) - b*focusastig_corrected[0] +c;

 



run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE"+scanrate);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 689"); 
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 2"); 


run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+-b/(2*a)); wait(50);

print(wd+ " "+ -b/(2*a)  + " " +optwd1x);
x[0]=x[1];y[0]=y[1];
if (isOpen("autocorr filter")){
selectWindow("autocorr filter");
close();
}
Plot.create("autocorr filter", "mm", "focus function", x, y); 

/* 	  
if (isOpen("std")){
selectWindow("std");
close();
}
Plot.create("std", "mm", "focus function", x, y2);  	  
 
 */
 	  
}












function autofocusLS(){
	
		
setBatchMode(true);
	


makefocusastigmasks(sisc*6,sisc*0.5,sisc*3,fxxsize);
 
globmeans[0]=getmean("maskfocusouter");
globmeans[1]=getmean("maskfocusinner");
globmeans[2]=getmean("maskxminus");
globmeans[3]=getmean("maskxplus");
globmeans[4]=getmean("maskyminus");
globmeans[5]=getmean("maskyplus");



var wd_steps=5; //number of wd steps.  must be odd
var wd_stepsize=0.01; //in mm

x=newArray(wd_steps+1);
y=newArray(wd_steps+1);
 

wd=wd_vec[tilecount];


run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y"); wait(20);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X"); wait(20);

beamshiftx=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_X", nResults-1);

run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 2770"); 
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1");

imagename="testfocus"+i+".tif";

		x[i]=wd+(i-(wd_steps+1)/2)*wd_stepsize;

		run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshiftynew); wait(60);
		run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftxnew); wait(60);	
		acquireimage(x[i],waittimewd,dirimagename); 
		computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
		y[i]=log(focusnormalized);
	//}
}
 

run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE6");
run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd); wait(100);

run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftx); wait(60);	
 
   
selectWindow("maskxminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskxplus");
close();    
selectWindow("maskyminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskyplus");
close();   
selectWindow("maskfocusinner");
close();
selectWindow("maskfocusouter");
close();

setBatchMode(false);


// http://www.codeproject.com/KB/recipes/QuadraticRegression.aspx

s21=0;s11=0;s01=0;s40=0;s30=0;s20=0;s10=0;s00=0;
for(i=1;i<=wd_steps;i=i+1){
	s21=s21+y[i]*pow(x[i],2);
	s11=s11+y[i]*x[i];
	s01=s01+y[i];
	s40=s40+pow(x[i],4);
	s30=s30+pow(x[i],3);
	s20=s20+pow(x[i],2);
	s10=s10+x[i];	
	s00=s00+1;
}		
D=s40*(s20*s00-s10*s10) - s30*(s30*s00-s10*s20) + s20*(s30*s10-s20*s20);
Da=s21*(s20*s00-s10*s10) - s11*(s30*s00-s10*s20) + s01*(s30*s10-s20*s20);
Db=s40*(s11*s00-s01*s10) - s30*(s21*s00-s01*s20) + s20*(s21*s10-s11*s20);
Dc=s40*(s20*s01-s10*s11) - s30*(s30*s01-s10*s21) + s20*(s30*s11-s20*s21);

a=Da/D;
b=Db/D;
c=Dc/D;

focusastig_corrected[0]=-b/(2*a);
opty = a*pow(focusastig_corrected[0],2) - b*focusastig_corrected[0] +c;

x[0]=x[1];y[0]=y[1];
if (isOpen("autocorr filter")){
selectWindow("autocorr filter");

close();
wait(100);
}

//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1");

}
 





























 




function autofocusastig(){

run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v DP_SCANRATE"); wait(50);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE5");
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 1"); 
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 2770");wait(100);
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_FRAME_TIME");

waittimewd=1.1*getResult("AP_FRAME_TIME", nResults-1);
scanrate=getResult("DP_SCANRATE", nResults-1);

	
setBatchMode(true);
	


makefocusastigmasks(sisc*6,sisc*0.5,sisc*3,fxxsize);
 
globmeans[0]=getmean("maskfocusouter");
globmeans[1]=getmean("maskfocusinner");
globmeans[2]=getmean("maskxminus");
globmeans[3]=getmean("maskxplus");
globmeans[4]=getmean("maskyminus");
globmeans[5]=getmean("maskyplus");


var wd_steps=3; //number of wd steps.  must be odd
var wd_stepsize=0.005; //in mm
var astig_stepsize=0.05; 

x=newArray(4);
x2=newArray(4);
x3=newArray(4);
y=newArray(4);
y2=newArray(4);
y3=newArray(4);

wd=wd_vec[tilecount];
astigx=astigx_vec[tilecount];
astigy=astigy_vec[tilecount];

for(i=1;i<=wd_steps;i=i+1){
	x[i]=wd+(i-(wd_steps+1)/2)*wd_stepsize;
	if(autoastig==0){
		astig_stepsize=0;
	}
	x2[i]=astigx+(i-(wd_steps+1)/2)*astig_stepsize;
	x3[i]=astigy+(i-(wd_steps+1)/2)*astig_stepsize;
	var imagename="testfocus"+i+".tif";
	var dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
	acquireimage(x[i],x2[i],x3[i],waittimewd,dirimagename); 
	computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
	y[i]=focusnormalized;
	if(autoastig==1){
		y2[i]=astigxnormalized;
		y3[i]=astigynormalized;
	}
}
 

 run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE6");
 run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd); wait(100);
  
   
selectWindow("maskfocusinner");
close();
selectWindow("maskfocusouter");
close();

setBatchMode(false);


focusastig_corrected[3]=focusastig_corrected[0];focusastig_corrected[4]=focusastig_corrected[1];focusastig_corrected[5]=focusastig_corrected[2];
	
a = ((y[2]-y[1])*(x[1]-x[3]) + (y[3]-y[1])*(x[2]-x[1])) / ((x[1]-x[3])*(pow(x[2],2)-pow(x[1],2)) + (x[2]-x[1])*(pow(x[3],2)-pow(x[1],2)));
b = ((y[2] - y[1]) - a*(pow(x[2],2) - pow(x[1],2))) / (x[2]-x[1]);
c =  y[1] - a*pow(x[1],2) - b*x[1];
focusastig_corrected[0]=-b/(2*a);
opty = a*pow(focusastig_corrected[0],2) - b*focusastig_corrected[0] +c;
if (a>0){
	//focusastig_corrected[0]=focusastig_corrected[3];
}
 
 
if(autoastig==1){ 
 
	a2 = ((y2[2]-y2[1])*(x2[1]-x2[3]) + (y2[3]-y2[1])*(x2[2]-x2[1])) / ((x2[1]-x2[3])*(pow(x2[2],2)-pow(x2[1],2)) + (x2[2]-x2[1])*(pow(x2[3],2)-pow(x2[1],2)));
	b2 = ((y2[2] - y2[1]) - a2*(pow(x2[2],2) - pow(x2[1],2))) / (x2[2]-x2[1]);
	c2 =  y2[1] - a2*pow(x2[1],2) - b2*x2[1];
	focusastig_corrected[1]=-b2/(2*a2);
	opty2 = a2*pow(focusastig_corrected[1],2) - b2*focusastig_corrected[1] +c2;

	a3 = ((y3[2]-y3[1])*(x3[1]-x3[3]) + (y3[3]-y3[1])*(x3[2]-x3[1])) / ((x3[1]-x3[3])*(pow(x3[2],2)-pow(x3[1],2)) + (x3[2]-x3[1])*(pow(x3[3],2)-pow(x3[1],2)));
	b3 = ((y3[2] - y3[1]) - a3*(pow(x3[2],2) - pow(x3[1],2))) / (x3[2]-x3[1]);
	c3 =  y3[1] - a3*pow(x3[1],2) - b3*x3[1];
	focusastig_corrected[2]=-b3/(2*a3);
	opty3 = a3*pow(focusastig_corrected[2],2) - b3*focusastig_corrected[2] +c3;

	if (a2>0){
		//focusastig_corrected[1]=focusastig_corrected[4];
	}
	if (a3>0){
		//focusastig_corrected[2]=focusastig_corrected[5];
	}


}





run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE"+scanrate);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 2"); 
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 689");wait(100);

}

	a = ((y[2]-y[1])*(x[1]-x[3]) + (y[3]-y[1])*(x[2]-x[1])) / ((x[1]-x[3])*(pow(x[2],2)-pow(x[1],2)) + (x[2]-x[1])*(pow(x[3],2)-pow(x[1],2)));

function autofocus(wd,ap_mag,wd_stepsize,scanspeed,fittype,focusmeasure,scanres){	 

setBatchMode(true);
	


makefocusastigmasks(sisc*6,sisc*0.5,sisc*3,fxxsize);
 
globmeans[0]=getmean("maskfocusouter");
globmeans[1]=getmean("maskfocusinner");
globmeans[2]=getmean("maskxminus");
globmeans[3]=getmean("maskxplus");
globmeans[4]=getmean("maskyminus");
globmeans[5]=getmean("maskyplus");



wd_steps=3;
//var wd_stepsize=0.008; //in mm

x=newArray(wd_steps+1);
y=newArray(wd_steps+1);
 

//wd=wd_vec[tilecount];


run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y"); wait(20);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X"); wait(20);	
beamshifty=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y", nResults-1);	
beamshiftx=getResult("AP_BEAMSHIFT_X", nResults-1);	
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v DP_SCANRATE"); wait(50);
scanrate=getResult("DP_SCANRATE", nResults-1);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE"+scanspeed);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE "+scanres);  //0 for 1024, 1 for 512
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG "+ap_mag); 
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); 
run("SEM ", "GetZeissNumericParameter v AP_FRAME_TIME");

waittimewd=1.1*getResult("AP_FRAME_TIME", nResults-1);

beamshiftynew=beamshifty+(random-0.5)*1;
beamshiftxnew=beamshiftx+(random-0.5)*1;
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshiftynew); wait(60);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftxnew); wait(60);	 

x[1]=wd-wd_stepsize/2;
imagename="testfocus1.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
acquireimage(x[1],waittimewd,dirimagename);
acquireimage(x[1],waittimewd,dirimagename);
if (focusmeasure==0){
	y[1]=computeWDfun2(dirnamewd,imagename);
}else if (focusmeasure==1){
	y[1]=computeVarfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
}else{
	y[1]=computeWDfun3(dirnamewd,imagename);
}

xmax=x[1];ymax=y[1];

beamshiftynew=beamshifty+(random-0.5)*1;
beamshiftxnew=beamshiftx+(random-0.5)*1;
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshiftynew); wait(60);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftxnew); wait(60);	 


//x[2]=wd+wd_stepsize/2;
x[2]=wd;
imagename="testfocus2.tif";
dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
acquireimage(x[2],waittimewd,dirimagename);


if (focusmeasure==0){
	y[2]=computeWDfun2(dirnamewd,imagename);
}else if (focusmeasure==1){
	y[2]=computeVarfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
}else{
	y[2]=computeWDfun3(dirnamewd,imagename);
}

 

if (y[2]>y[1]){
	
		//x[3]=wd+3*wd_stepsize/2;
		x[3]=wd+wd_stepsize;
		xmax=x[2];
		ymax=y[2];
}else{
		//x[3]=wd-3*wd_stepsize/2;
		x[3]=wd-2*wd_stepsize;
}
		imagename="testfocus3.tif";
		dirimagename=dirnamewd+imagename;
		acquireimage(x[3],waittimewd,dirimagename);
		if (focusmeasure==0){
			y[3]=computeWDfun2(dirnamewd,imagename);
		}else if (focusmeasure==1){
			y[3]=computeVarfun(dirnamewd,imagename);
		}else{
			y[3]=computeWDfun3(dirnamewd,imagename);
		}

if (y[3]>ymax){	 
		xmax=x[3]; ymax=y[3];
} 
 

run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE6");
//run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd); wait(100);
//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_Y "+beamshifty); wait(60);
//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_BEAMSHIFT_X "+beamshiftx); wait(60);	
 
   
selectWindow("maskxminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskxplus");
close();    
selectWindow("maskyminus");
close(); 
selectWindow("maskyplus");
close();   
selectWindow("maskfocusinner");
close();
selectWindow("maskfocusouter");
close();

setBatchMode(false);


// http://www.codeproject.com/KB/recipes/QuadraticRegression.aspx

s21=0;s11=0;s01=0;s40=0;s30=0;s20=0;s10=0;s00=0;
for(i=1;i<=wd_steps;i=i+1){
	s21=s21+y[i]*pow(x[i],2);
	s11=s11+y[i]*x[i];
	s01=s01+y[i];
	s40=s40+pow(x[i],4);
	s30=s30+pow(x[i],3);
	s20=s20+pow(x[i],2);
	s10=s10+x[i];	
	s00=s00+1;
}		
D=s40*(s20*s00-s10*s10) - s30*(s30*s00-s10*s20) + s20*(s30*s10-s20*s20);
Da=s21*(s20*s00-s10*s10) - s11*(s30*s00-s10*s20) + s01*(s30*s10-s20*s20);
Db=s40*(s11*s00-s01*s10) - s30*(s21*s00-s01*s20) + s20*(s21*s10-s11*s20);
Dc=s40*(s20*s01-s10*s11) - s30*(s30*s01-s10*s21) + s20*(s30*s11-s20*s21);

a=Da/D;
b=Db/D;
c=Dc/D;

focusastig_corrected[0]=-b/(2*a);
opty = a*pow(focusastig_corrected[0],2) - b*focusastig_corrected[0] +c;

x[0]=x[1];y[0]=y[1];
if (isOpen("autocorr filter")){
selectWindow("autocorr filter");

close();
wait(100);
} 

Plot.create("autocorr filter", "mm "+focusastig_corrected[0], "focus function", x, y); 
 
Plot.show();
saveAs("PNG", "D:\\Dropbox\\autocorrs\\autocorr"+tilecount+".png");
close();

run("SEM ", "SetZeissStringParameter v CMD_SCANRATE"+scanrate);
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_IMAGE_STORE 2"); 
run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v AP_MAG 689");
//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); 
wait(40);

if (fittype==0){
	return focusastig_corrected[0];
}else{
	return xmax;
}

}

	function makefocusastigmasks(a,b,c,size){
	//print("makefocusmasks");
	//--the masks are differences of gaussians 
	//--with the inner mask exp(-r^2/c)-exp(-r^2/b)
	//--and the out mask exp(-r^2/a)-exp(-r^2/c)
	//-- a=5; // 
	//-- b=1;
	//-- c=3;
	newImage("maskfocusinner", "8-bit Black", size, size, 1);
	setLocation(0, 0);
	for (i=0; i < size; i++) {
		for (j=0; j < size; j++){
			x=i-size/2;
			y=j-size/2;
			r=sqrt(x*x + y*y);
			cosphi=y/r;
			sinphi=x/r;
			setPixel(i, j, 256*(exp(-(r*r)/c)-exp(-(r*r)/b)));
			};
		};
	newImage("maskfocusouter", "8-bit Black", size, size, 1);
	setLocation(0, 0);
	for (i=0; i < size; i++) {
		for (j=0; j < size; j++){
			x=i-size/2;
			y=j-size/2;
			r=sqrt(x*x + y*y);
			cosphi=y/r;
			sinphi=x/r;
			setPixel(i, j, 256*(exp(-(r*r)/a)-exp(-(r*r)/c)));
			};
		};

	newImage("maskxplus", "8-bit Black", size, size, 1);
	setLocation(0, 0);
	for (i=0; i < size; i++) {
		for (j=0; j < size; j++){
			x=i-size/2;
			y=j-size/2;
			r=sqrt(x*x + y*y);
			cosphi=y/r;
			sinphi=x/r;
			setPixel(i, j, 256*cosphi*cosphi*(exp(-(r*r)/a)-exp(-(r*r)/b)));
			};
		};
	newImage("maskxminus", "8-bit Black", size, size, 1);
	setLocation(0, 0);
	for (i=0; i < size; i++) {
		for (j=0; j < size; j++){
			x=i-size/2;
			y=j-size/2;
			r=sqrt(x*x + y*y);
			cosphi=y/r;
			sinphi=x/r;
			setPixel(i, j, 256*sinphi*sinphi*(exp(-(r*r)/a)-exp(-(r*r)/b)));
			};
		};
	newImage("maskyplus", "8-bit Black", size, size, 1);
	setLocation(0, 0);
	for (i=0; i < size; i++) {
		for (j=0; j < size; j++){
			x=i-size/2;
			y=j-size/2;
			r=sqrt(x*x + y*y);
			cosphi=y/r;
			sinphi=x/r;
			setPixel(i, j, 128*(sinphi+cosphi)*(sinphi+cosphi)*(exp(-(r*r)/a)-exp(-(r*r)/b)));
			};
		};
	newImage("maskyminus", "8-bit Black", size, size, 1);
	setLocation(0, 0);
	for (i=0; i < size; i++) {
		for (j=0; j < size; j++){
			x=i-size/2;
			y=j-size/2;
			r=sqrt(x*x + y*y);
			cosphi=y/r;
			sinphi=x/r;
			setPixel(i, j, 128*(sinphi-cosphi)*(sinphi-cosphi)*(exp(-(r*r)/a)-exp(-(r*r)/b)));
			};
		};
	};











	
function getmean(window){
	selectWindow(window);
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
	return mean;
	};
	
	
function acquireimage(wd2,waittime,filename){
	run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd2); wait(10);
	//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); wait(10);
	run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 0"); wait(10);
	//run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); 
	wait(waittime+100); 
	run("SEM ", "FileSave v "+filename);wait(50);
}
	
function acquireimage2(wd2,astigx2,astigy2,waittime,filename){
	run("SEM ", "SetFreeWorkingDistance v  "+wd2); wait(100);
	run("SEM ", "SetStigmator v "+astigx2+" "+astigy2); 
	run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); wait(100);
	run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 0"); wait(100);
	run("SEM ", "SetZeissNumericParameter v DP_FROZEN 1"); wait(100);
	wait(waittime+100); 
	run("SEM ", "FileSave v "+filename);wait(100);
}









function computeVarfun(dirnamewd,imagename){
 n=1;
 
 open(dirnamewd + imagename);
run("Median...", "radius=.5");
getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
 close();

	
	return std;
	

}



















function computeWDfun3(dirnamewd,imagename){   
 
 
 open(dirnamewd + imagename);
 run("Variance...", "radius=2");
 getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
 imagemean=mean;
 close();
 
return imagemean;

}



function computeWDfun2(dirnamewd,imagename){   //for 1024 size images
 
 
 open(dirnamewd + imagename);

	run("Select All");
	imheight=getHeight();
	imwidth=getWidth();
	run("Copy");
	
	run("Scale...", "x=1 y=1 create title=centerofcc1");
	selectWindow("centerofcc1");
	run("Paste");
	makeRectangle(0,0,512,512);
	run("Crop");
	
	selectWindow(imagename);
	run("Scale...", "x=1 y=1 create title=centerofcc2");
	selectWindow("centerofcc2");
	run("Paste");
	makeRectangle(0,imheight-512,512,512);
	run("Crop");
	
	selectWindow(imagename);
	run("Scale...", "x=1 y=1 create title=centerofcc3");
	selectWindow("centerofcc3");
	run("Paste");
	makeRectangle(imwidth-512,0,512,512);
	run("Crop");
	
	selectWindow(imagename);
	run("Scale...", "x=1 y=1 create title=centerofcc4");
	selectWindow("centerofcc4");
	run("Paste");
	makeRectangle(imwidth-512,imheight-512,512,512);
	run("Crop");
	
	selectWindow(imagename);
	run("Scale...", "x=1 y=1 create title=centerofcc5");
	selectWindow("centerofcc5");
	run("Paste");
	makeRectangle(imwidth/4,imheight/4,512,512);
	run("Crop");
	
	
	
	focusvals=newArray(5);
	
	for (i=1; i <= 5; i++) {
	
	

	run("FD Math...", "image1=centerofcc"+i+" operation=Correlate image2=centerofcc"+i+" result=cc"+i+" do");
	selectWindow("centerofcc"+i);
	close();
	selectWindow("cc"+i);

		
	ccsize=getHeight();
	makeRectangle(ccsize/2-fxxsize/2,ccsize/2-fxxsize/2, fxxsize, fxxsize);
	run("Crop");
 
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
 
	imagemean=mean;
 
	imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+i,"maskfocusinner");
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
	innercoeff=mean/globmeans[1];
	close();	
	imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+i,"maskfocusouter");
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
	outercoeff=mean/globmeans[0];
	close();
	//focuscoeff=innercoeff-outercoeff;
	
	//focusnormalized=focuscoeff/(innercoeff+outercoeff-2*fxxsize*fxxsize*imagemean*imagemean);
	focusnormalized=(innercoeff-outercoeff)/(innercoeff+outercoeff);
	//print(innercoeff+" "+outercoeff+" "+focuscoeff);
	
	selectWindow("cc"+i);
	close();
	
	focusvals[i-1]=focusnormalized;
	//print(focusnormalized+" "+innercoeff+" "+outercoeff);
	//print(focusnormalized);
	
	}
	 
	//print(focusvals[2]);
	
	
	focusvals=Array.sort(focusvals);
	
	//print(focusvals[2]);
	
	
	selectWindow(imagename);
	close();
	
	//print(focusvals[0]+" "+focusvals[1]+" "+focusvals[2]+" "+focusvals[3]+" "+focusvals[4]);
	return focusvals[4];
	//y1=focuscoeff;
	
	
	
	
}

































function computeWDfun(dirnamewd,imagename){
 n=1;
 
 open(dirnamewd + imagename);

	run("Select All");
	run("Copy");
	
	run("Scale...", "x=1 y=1 create title=centerofcc");
	selectWindow("centerofcc");
	run("Paste");
	imheight=getHeight();
	imwidth=getWidth();
	makeRectangle(imwidth/2-256/2,imheight/2-256/2, 256, 256);
	run("Crop");

	run("FD Math...", "image1=centerofcc operation=Correlate image2=centerofcc result=cc"+n+" do");
	selectWindow("centerofcc");
	close();
	selectWindow("cc"+n);

		
	ccsize=getHeight();
	makeRectangle(ccsize/2-fxxsize/2,ccsize/2-fxxsize/2, fxxsize, fxxsize);
	run("Crop");
 
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
 
	imagemean=mean;
 
	imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskfocusinner");
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
	innercoeff=mean/globmeans[1];
	close();	
	imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskfocusouter");
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
	outercoeff=mean/globmeans[0];
	close();
	focuscoeff=innercoeff-outercoeff;
	focusnormalized=focuscoeff/(innercoeff+outercoeff-2*fxxsize*fxxsize*imagemean*imagemean);
	focusnormalized=(innercoeff-outercoeff)/(innercoeff+outercoeff);
	//print(innercoeff+" "+outercoeff+" "+focuscoeff);
	
	selectWindow("cc"+n);
	close();
	selectWindow(imagename);
	close();
	
	return focusnormalized;
	//y1=focuscoeff;
	
	
	
	
}





function computeFocusAstigfun(dirnamewd,imagename){
 n=1;
 
 open(dirnamewd + imagename);
 //run("Median...", "radius=1.5");

	run("Select All");
	run("Copy");
	
	run("Scale...", "x=1 y=1 create title=centerofcc");
	selectWindow("centerofcc");
	run("Paste");
	imheight=getHeight();
	imwidth=getWidth();
	makeRectangle(imwidth/2-256/2,imheight/2-256/2, 256, 256);
	run("Crop");

	run("FD Math...", "image1=centerofcc operation=Correlate image2=centerofcc result=cc"+n+" do");
	selectWindow("centerofcc");
	close();
	selectWindow("cc"+n);

		
	ccsize=getHeight();
	makeRectangle(ccsize/2-fxxsize/2,ccsize/2-fxxsize/2, fxxsize, fxxsize);
	run("Crop");
 
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
 
	imagemean=mean;
	

	imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskfocusouter");
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
	outercoeff=mean/globmeans[0];
	close(); 
	imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskfocusinner");
	getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
	innercoeff=mean/globmeans[1];
	close();	
	focusnormalized=(innercoeff-outercoeff)/(innercoeff+outercoeff);
	
	if(autoastig==1){
		imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskxminus");
		getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
		xminuscoeff=mean/globmeans[2];
		close();	
		imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskxplus");
		getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
		xpluscoeff=mean/globmeans[3];
		close();
		imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskyminus");
		getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
		yminuscoeff=mean/globmeans[4];
		close();	
		imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "cc"+n,"maskyplus");
		getRawStatistics(nPixels, mean, min, max, std, histogram);
		ypluscoeff=mean/globmeans[5];
		close();	
		astigxnormalized=(xpluscoeff-xminuscoeff)/(xpluscoeff+xminuscoeff);
		astigynormalized=(ypluscoeff-yminuscoeff)/(ypluscoeff+yminuscoeff);
	}
	
	
	selectWindow("cc"+n);
	close();
	selectWindow(imagename);
	close();
	
	
	
}

function closeWindows(wname) {
	while (isOpen(wname)) {selectWindow(wname);close();};
	};


function formatcubeInt(x){

if (x<10)
return "000"+x;
else if (x<100)
return "00"+x;
else if (x<1000)
return "0"+x;
else if (x<10000)
return x;
else return x;
};

function printArray(a) {
      print("");
      for (i=0; i<a.length; i++)
          print(i+": "+a[i]);
  }

  function computePlane(x1,y1,w1,x2,y2,w2,x3,y3,w3) {
  //print(x1+" " +y1+" " +w1+" " +x2+" " +y2+" " +w2+" " +x3+" " +y3+" " +w3);
A = y1*(w2 - w3) + y2*(w3 - w1) + y3*(w1 - w2);
B = w1*(x2 - x3) + w2*(x3 - x1) + w3*(x1 - x2);
C = x1*(y2 - y3) + x2*(y3 - y1) + x3*(y1 - y2);
D = -x1*(y2*w3 - y3*w2) - x2*(y3*w1 - y1*w3) - x3*(y1*w2 - y2*w1);
//print(A+" " +B);
  }

function sendEmail (message, recipient, sender){
	for (i=0; i<recipient.length;i++){
		run("Send Email", recipient[i]+" SEM_control "+message+" "+sender);};
	};

function sendEmail2 (message, recipient, sender,attachstr){
	for (i=0; i<recipient.length;i++){
		run("Send Email", recipient[i]+" SEM_control "+message+" "+sender+" "+attachstr);};
	};
